-Since enacting sanctions, Iran’s crude exports have fallen off, the value of Iran’s currency has plummeted, and international companies have pulled out of the country.

THREAD CONTINUED: All of President Trump's national security accomplishments from the last 2 years:
-ICE rescued or identified over 500 human trafficking victims and over 900 child exploitation victims in 2017 alone.
-ICE removed over 226,000 illegal aliens from the United States in 2017.
-Enhanced vetting of individuals entering the U.S. from countries that don’t meet security standards, helping to ensure individuals who pose a threat to our country are identified before they enter.	These procedures were upheld in a June 2018 Supreme Court hearing
-Authorized the deployment of the National Guard to help secure the border.
-Released an immigration framework that includes the resources required to secure our borders and close legal loopholes, and repeatedly called on Congress to fix our broken immigration laws.
-DOJ launched their Joint Criminal Opioid Darknet Enforcement (J-CODE) team, aimed at disrupting online illicit opioid sales.
-DOJ secured its first-ever indictments against Chinese fentanyl manufacturers.
-Signed the INTERDICT Act into law, enhancing efforts to detect and intercept synthetic opioids.
-Stop Opioid Abuse and Reduce Drug Supply and Demand introduced new measures to keep dangerous drugs out the United States.
-ICE HSI made 11,691 narcotics-related arrests in FY 2017.
-ICE HSI dedicated nearly 630,000 investigative hours towards halting the illegal import of fentanyl.
-ICE HSI seized more than 980,000 pounds of narcotics in FY 2017, including 2,370 pounds of fentanyl and 6,967 pounds of heroin.
-Border Patrol agents arrested 228 illegal aliens affiliated with MS-13 in FY 2017.
-Justice worked with partners in Central America to secure criminal charges against more than 4,000 MS-13 members.
-ICE’s Homeland Security Investigations division arrested 796 MS-13 members and associates in FY 2017, an 83 percent increase from the prior year.
-Worked to protect American communities from the threat posed by the vile MS-13 gang.
-Construction of a 14-mile section of border wall began near San Diego.
-Secured $1.6 billion for border wall construction in the March 2018 omnibus bill.
